Local News

Zhang Qun Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning from Nanjing 105

Spoke about diplomatic policy as in previous speeches

Foreign Minister Zhang Qun, accompanied by Chen Jie, the permanent director of the Foreign Ministry, Li Dijun, the director of the Intelligence Department, and Secretary Duan Guanhai, left Nanjing on the 11:00 PM express train the night before last and arrived at the North Station in Shanghai at around 7:00 AM yesterday morning. Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of the city, representing Li Dachao, Yang Hu, the commander of the Songhu Garrison, representing Wang Zhinan, Cai Jingjun, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Zhou Jue, the director of the Foreign Ministry's Shanghai Office, went to the train station to greet him.

After getting off the train, Zhang returned to his private residence on Avenue Albert to rest. At 10:15 AM, he drove with his wife to Avenue Petain to visit Huang Fu, the former chairman of the Executive Yuan's Political Reorganization Committee in Pingjin, for a long talk and stayed for lunch at Huang's residence. It is said that Zhang not only inquired about Huang's long-standing illness but also solicited Huang's opinions on foreign policy.

Schedule in Shanghai. Later, at 5:00 PM, he went to the municipal government in the city center to attend a grand tea party hosted by Mayor Wu to meet with ambassadors, envoys, charges d'affaires, consuls general, and military attachés from various countries in Shanghai. Zhang also scheduled to attend the annual social gathering of the Institute of International Affairs at the International Hotel from 6:00 PM to 8:00 PM tomorrow night and deliver a speech. The day after tomorrow will be spent visiting friends and resting. He is scheduled to return to Nanjing on the 11:00 PM express train the night after the day after tomorrow.

Zhang's Remarks. A reporter from the Central News Agency met Foreign Minister Zhang at the North Station yesterday morning and inquired about diplomacy with Japan. According to Zhang, his diplomatic policy was announced in his speech at the Foreign Ministry's memorial week last Monday. We can only move forward on the path of self-confidence with the greatest effort. As for the negotiations on increasing troops in North China and the smuggling issue, the progress has been reported in the newspapers, and there are currently no new developments.

Municipal Government Tea Party Last Night 106

Hosted Minister Zhang and His Wife and Chinese and Foreign Guests

The Shanghai Municipal Government hosted a gathering of Chinese and foreign guests from all walks of life in the city yesterday to strengthen friendship. From 5:00 PM to 7:00 PM, Mayor Wu and his wife held this year's spring tea party in the Municipal Government Auditorium, hosting Minister Zhang of the Foreign Ministry and his wife, ambassadors, ministers, charges d'affaires, military commanders, military attachés, consuls general, and Chinese and foreign guests from all walks of life, totaling about 1,800 people. Mayor Wu and his wife, as well as senior officials of the municipal government, warmly greeted them and introduced them to Minister Zhang and his wife. The guests and hosts toasted and chatted happily, and the area in the city center was bustling with traffic, a grand scene for a time.

The Situation is Peaceful and Stable Shanghai's Financial Situation is Stable 107

Interbank lending rates are calm, bill exchange is sharply increasing, foreign exchange is stable, and national banks are supplying as much as possible. Bond prices in the stock exchange are rising across the board.

The New News Agency reports that although some unfounded rumors have been circulating in the Shanghai financial market, the financial market is still very stable. Securities trading has rebounded across the board. Although the interbank lending rate of the Money Trade Association has risen by one point compared to the previous week, this is purely due to supply and demand and is not affected by rumors. The public single lending rate and the acceptance bill discount rate of the Bank United Reserve Association are the same as the previous week. Although foreign exchange has fluctuated slightly, the changes are very small. The details are as follows:

Interbank Lending Rates are Calm as Usual

The financial market in the city has been generally calm since this week. The interbank lending rate opened by the Money Trade Association has been at 9 points except on Sunday, but it has risen by one point compared to last week. This is because the demand for cash this week is slightly higher, which is entirely due to the relationship between supply and demand. The public single lending rate opened by the Bank United Reserve Committee has always been listed at one dime (10 cents), and the discount rate for its acceptance bills has also not changed, remaining at one dime and two points (12 cents). This shows a glimpse of the financial stability of Shanghai.

Bill Exchange Volume Increases Sharply

The total amount of bill exchange in the banking and money industries in this port has increased sharply compared to last week. The total amount of exchange in the Banking Association is 374,293,057.72 yuan in national currency, an increase of 166,841,179.66 yuan compared to the previous period of 207,451,878.06 yuan. The exchange volume, transfer volume, and total collection volume also increased sharply like the total amount. The total amount of bill exchange in the Money Trade Association this week was 310,902,500 yuan, an increase of 27,558,000 yuan compared to the previous period of 293,344,500 yuan.

Foreign Exchange Market is Slightly Active

The foreign exchange market in Shanghai this week has been slightly active. The near-term price of British exchange is 1 shilling, 2 pence, and 375 points. The amount purchased at this price is quite large, but the national banks are supplying as much as possible to stabilize it. Therefore, British exchange has always stood firm at the selling price of the Central Bank. The forward price of British exchange is tightening. On Thursday, the British exchange for June shrank from 1 shilling, 2 pence, and 34375 points to 1 shilling, 2 pence, and 3125 points, and the July term shrank from 1 shilling, 2 pence, and 3125 points to 28125 points. As for the US exchange, it has become looser. The near-term price has increased from 29 yuan and 8125 points to 29 yuan and 875 points. From Wednesday, the forward price has increased by 0625 points for each month. On Friday, the price of the US exchange for June reached 29 yuan and 8125 points, and the July term reached 29 yuan and 75 points. The reason for the tightening of foreign exchange this week is entirely due to the collusion between Japanese banks and Chinese merchants, and the relatively tight financial situation at the end of the month also has an impact. However, pure commercial transactions this week are relatively rare, while bank-to-bank transactions and speculative trading are more prosperous.

The Amount of Legal Tender Issued Has Increased

According to the inspection report on Saturday, the amount issued by the Central Bank is 277,775,264 yuan, an increase of 1,710,460 yuan compared to the previous period of 276,064,836 yuan. The cash reserve has also increased considerably, namely 982,828 yuan. As for the amount issued by the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, according to the Sixth Inspection Report of the Issuing Reserve Committee, the former is 343,155,286 yuan and the latter is 201,401,740 yuan, and the cash reserves are also maintained at a considerable level.

Customs Prevents Smuggling 108

Specially Appointed Customs Officers to be Stationed at Stations for Inspection

In order to prevent smuggling by road transport, the Jianghai Customs has issued a notice stipulating the method of obtaining tax-paid certificates, which has been implemented since the 3rd of this month. The first notice issued by Ansier, the director of the Chief Inspectorate, is recorded as follows: According to the notice issued by the Inspector General of Customs and approved by the Executive Yuan on measures to prevent smuggling by road transport, we are instructed to comply with it immediately, etc. According to the regulations of the aforementioned measures, all foreign goods transported by railway must have a tax-paid certificate issued by the customs; otherwise, the railway bureau will refuse to transport them. In the future, if foreign goods listed in the attached list are transported by railway without this certificate, they may be seized by the customs officers stationed at the arrival station. Merchants can obtain this certificate free of charge from the customs where the goods were originally imported or re-exported by presenting various documents for import duties that have been paid. The goods listed in the attached table may be changed at any time depending on the circumstances. In addition to the procedures for applying for the certificate, which will be announced by the Customs Tax Department, this notice is hereby issued for general knowledge. This notice, Director Ansier (attached table omitted).

The Shanghai North and South Stations of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, and the McGonaghy Road Freight Station, are the overall hubs of Shanghai's vehicle transport and are extremely important. The Jianghai Customs specially appointed Yaleson, the Western Chief Inspector, yesterday to lead customs officers to establish inspection offices at the above stations. Six customs officers were stationed at each office, rotating regularly to inspect smuggled goods, and railway police cooperated in handling the matter. When necessary, they could inspect the vehicles and deal with them strictly.

Industry and Commerce Loan Association Approved Loan Yesterday 109

Totaling 12,350 yuan

The Shanghai Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee held its 30th meeting at the Bank of China National Goods in Tianjin Road at half past noon on the day of this month. The committee members present were Cai Zengji, Qin Runqing, Song Ziliang, Yu Zuoyan, Du Yuesheng, (Yu acting for) Wang Xiaolai, Bei Songsun, (Wang acting for) Wu Xingya, and (Wu Huanru acting for) the aforementioned gentlemen. Chairman Cai Zengji reported on the routine affairs of the meeting and then presented thirty-one applications for small credit loans. After review and decision, one company was approved for half of the original application amount, and thirty companies were approved for a reduced amount, for a total loan of 12,350 yuan. In addition, five companies were rejected for loans because their business activities were inconsistent with the loan principles or because the loan applications were inconsistent with the regulations. All reviewed cases will be notified to the respective applicants by the association. According to the three loan principles set by the Ministry of Finance, all factories that sell domestic goods, transport domestic goods for export, and manufacture domestic goods can apply for loans from the association without the need for any introduction. Recently, it has been reported that some cunning people have taken advantage of the ignorance of merchants and used the excuse of introducing loans to take the opportunity to make profits. It is also said that there are not a few who have been deceived, but no conclusive evidence has been obtained. It is also heard that the association is strictly investigating this matter in order to eliminate this malpractice as much as possible and to facilitate merchants. It is hoped that factories that want to apply for loans in the future will pay close attention. If there is any uncertainty about the loan procedures, they should go to the association's office on the upper floor of the Bank of China National Goods on Tianjin Road to inquire and avoid being deceived by villains.

Thirteen Fishmongers Joined the Fish Market Today 110

Officially Replied to Comply with Guidance to Join Cooperation. Mediators Accompanied Fishmonger Representatives to Participate.

The dispute between the fish market and the thirteen fishmongers who had not joined the fish market has been resolved since the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association convened representatives of the fishmongers on the 2nd of this month to provide guidance. Yesterday, the Yongxian Fish Industry Association officially replied, expressing compliance with the guidance and agreeing to join. According to the letter, in addition to forwarding it to the fish market and conveying the opinions of the fishmongers, the association has scheduled mediators such as Yu Qiaqing to accompany the representatives of the thirteen fishmongers to participate this afternoon. The details are recorded below:

Fishmongers Comply with Guidance

The Yongxian Fish Industry Association sent a letter to the Ningbo Fellow Association yesterday, saying, "Dear Sirs, We have received your letter, and we are grateful for the earnest persuasion of village heads Qiaqing, Tingsun, Zuoting, and Yanfang to join the fish market. Our association convened a meeting of all members, and they all agreed that since you have sincerely mediated and promised to be responsible for the solution, our members will follow your instructions and join with pain. However, we ask that you expedite the requests mentioned and make every effort to resolve them so as to achieve a satisfactory result, maintain the release of funds from each line, preserve equal treatment, and ensure the livelihoods of employees. When and what day will be scheduled, and when will we enter the market for business? We will wait for your consideration. Please check the letter, etc. and reply immediately. Sincerely, the Shanghai Ice Fresh Fish Industry Association, affiliated with the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association."

Three Points in the Forwarded Letter

After receiving the letter, the Fellow Association sent a letter to the fish market, saying, "Dear Sirs, Regarding the matter of the thirteen fishmongers in Xiaodongmen who have not joined your market for business, after repeated persuasion by our association, there is a possibility of cooperation. However, the hopes of the fishmongers are to preserve the release of funds from each line, equal treatment with the fishmongers who joined earlier, and to take care of the livelihoods of employees. Therefore, we hereby inform you of the situation and hope that your association will convene a director to ask this association to invite representatives of the fishmongers to accompany them to the meeting for formal participation. Please check and handle the matter and reply immediately. Sincerely, to the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Fish Market."

Accompanied to Participate

The Fellow Association sent a letter to the Ice Fresh Fish Industry Association, instructing the fishmongers to each appoint a representative to accompany the mediators to participate in the cooperation. The letter said, "Dear Sirs, We have received your reply and are very grateful. Our association has already informed the fish market to check and handle the matter. The fish market has scheduled a joint meeting of the directors and supervisors at 2:00 PM on the 5th of this month. Please quickly notify the thirteen fishmongers of your association to each send a representative to the association at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 5th, accompanied by Yu Qiaqing, Yu Zuoting, Fang Jiaobo, and Zhang Shenzhi, to participate in the cooperation. Therefore, we hereby reply and hope that you will check and handle the matter accordingly. Sincerely, to the Ice Fresh Fish Industry Association."

Market Meeting

The fish market issued a circular for the joint meeting of the directors and supervisors to be held this afternoon, as follows: "Dear Sirs, We have scheduled a joint meeting of the directors and supervisors to be held at 3:00 PM on June 5 (Friday) on the first floor of Zhonghui. Please check and attend at the time. Sincerely, the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Fish Market."

Communication Between Red and White Russian Communities 113

The Foreign Review translates the Shanghai Daily News as saying that recently, various groups of Red Russians belonging to the Soviet Consulate General have begun to actively communicate with powerful groups of White Russians. Among them, the "League of Young Russians" has followed the Soviet Union in chanting anti-Japanese slogans and has published "The Psychology of Russian Youth." Also, White Russians from Manchuria want to join the White Russians in the headquarters of the White Russians due to the expulsion of the Semenov faction of White Russians in Manchuria. In order to rescue the White Russians in Manchuria, there is also an anti-Japanese movement in Paris, which, in addition to distributing leaflets and giving speeches, will also petition the League of Nations to protect their lives and property.

Nine Provinces and Ten Mayors Long-Distance Telephone Calls Officially to Commence in September 114

Ministry of Communications Purchased 120 Amplifiers to be Distributed to Various Bureaus

In order to complete the national transportation network, the Ministry of Communications plans to lay long-distance telephone lines to nine provinces, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, Henan, Shandong, and Hebei, and ten mayors, including Nanjing, Shanghai, Beijing, Tianjin, Qingdao, Jinan, Wuhan, Hangzhou, Chongqing, and Changsha. Since work began last year, most of the work has been completed. Due to raw materials, the remaining work has not been able to open calls according to the original schedule. Reporters from the New News Agency learned from various sources yesterday that the entire project can be completed in three months, trial calls can be made in August, and the official call period will be in September. At the same time, the Ministry of Communications has ordered 120 amplifiers, which will be distributed to various bureaus for use after the long-distance lines of the provinces and mayors are completed.

Japan Increases Troops in North China and Protects Smuggling. Various Organizations Telegraph the Central Government for Negotiations, Requesting That a Serious Protest Be Lodged with the Japanese Side, Striving to Achieve the Goal of Ensuring Sovereignty and Integrity. 117

Although our side has repeatedly negotiated with Japan regarding the increase of troops in North China and the protection of smugglers, it has not been effective. Various organizations, including the General Labor Union of the city, telegraphed the central government yesterday, requesting that a serious protest be lodged with the Japanese side, striving to achieve the goal of ensuring sovereignty and integrity. The details are recorded below:

General Labor Union Telegram

The General Labor Union of the city telegraphed the central government yesterday, writing, "To the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government of Nanjing: Japan, under the pretext of the Boxer Protocol, protects overseas Chinese and increases troops in North China, obstructs customs officers from cracking down on smuggling, hinders our country's sovereignty, and destroys our country's finances. Although the government has repeatedly negotiated seriously, the results have not been achieved due to the Japanese side's strong attitude. According to Articles 7 and 9 of the Boxer Protocol, countries are only allowed to station troops in Beijing and along the Pingyu Railway to protect the safety of the embassies. It was not originally for the purpose of protecting overseas Chinese, so there is no need to station heavy troops. The fact that countries such as Britain, the United States, France, and Italy have never stationed heavy troops in Beijing and Tianjin is not difficult to see. Now that the embassies in Beijing and the transportation in Tianjin are not in any danger, they want to use this as an excuse to station heavy troops. Sima Zhao's intentions are known to everyone. Regarding the smuggling incident in North China, although the Japanese are trying to cover up the world with all kinds of sophistry, the facts are all there and cannot be denied. In short, Japan, under the name of the Boxer Protocol and the Tanggu Truce, is actually destroying sovereignty and protecting smuggling, trying to threaten the government. We hereby urgently telegraph you (the Yuan and the Ministry) to argue according to reason and strive to achieve the goal of withdrawing troops and ensuring the integrity of sovereignty. With the utmost urgency. Zhou Xuexiang, acting chairman of the Shanghai General Labor Union, and standing committee members Li Mengnan, Shao Xubai, Zhang Kechang, Long Peiyun, and Ye Xiang, respectfully."

Municipal Farmers' Association Telegram

(Abbreviated title) The news that Japan has increased troops in North China and protected smuggling has spread and shocked the country. Japan's increase of troops in North China is based on the pretext of the Boxer Protocol, using the name of protecting overseas Chinese and practicing the reality of coercion. The intention is obvious. Moreover, the various clauses contained in the Boxer Protocol are based on the situation at that time, so there are regulations to adapt to the situation, station troops in Beijing and along the Pingyu Railway, and protect embassies and overseas Chinese. There is no need to station heavy troops as if facing a great enemy. Moreover, times have changed, and it should not be forced to argue, to splice, to invoke the treaty, and to deceive oneself and others. In view of the fact that countries such as Britain, the United States, France, and Italy have never strongly supported the treaty and stationed heavy troops in Beijing and Tianjin, while the overseas Chinese are still living in peace, this proves that Japan's sudden increase in troops must be for other purposes. At a time when Sino-Japanese relations are gradually improving, it is a hindrance to promoting good relations. As for the issue of smuggling, it has a huge impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood. Tianjin is a major town in North China and a commercial hub. At present, smuggling in North China is becoming increasingly serious, and national tax revenue has been sharply reduced as a result. Not only will the national finances suffer losses, but the people of the whole country will also suffer. I dare to telegraph you (the Yuan) to ask you to lodge a serious protest with Japan in accordance with the law and to show the facts to friendly countries and await public opinion. I am waiting for your orders. Respectfully, the Shanghai Farmers' Association."

Issued a Declaration

The association issued a declaration yesterday, roughly stating that Japan is obstructing our customs from cracking down on smuggling, resulting in the rampant smuggling of goods in the market, which is enough to lead our industry and commerce to bankruptcy. After repeated negotiations, there have been no results. However, the Japanese side claims that it is based on the Tanggu Agreement. The Sino-Japanese Treaty of Commerce stipulates that there are strict regulations to prevent smuggling at all ports of commerce, and the anti-smuggling is under the jurisdiction of the customs police, which is different from the nature of the military and should not be subject to the Tanggu Agreement. Recently, it has borrowed words to protect overseas Chinese and increase troops in North China, claiming to be based on the Boxer Protocol. This treaty is purely for the safety of the embassies and cannot be used to protect overseas Chinese, and the responsibility for protecting overseas Chinese has been clearly stipulated in the Treaty of Commerce and rests with our country. Therefore, this move is purely without reason. (New News Agency)

Wireless Telephone Station Completed in Hankou: Shanghai-Hankou Trial Calls Begin, Official Opening Awaits Ministry's Decision 118

The Hankou domestic wireless telephone station, after the Ministry of Communications established an engineering office and determined Lujiadun, Zhanggong Dike, as the base for the station, has been under construction since the year before last. It was originally expected to be completed around November of last year, but the initial construction work was washed away by a major flood, causing the project to be delayed. After the floodwaters receded, construction was resumed, and the entire project was completed at the end of last month. The equipment has been installed, and the office has notified the Ministry of Communications International Wireless Radio Station on Renji Road in this city to prepare for the opening of trial calls between the two sides. The domestic wireless telephone in the Shanghai Zhenru Wireless Transceiver Station has already exchanged trial calls with the Hankou Lujiadun station since the early morning, with excellent results. Once the Ministry decides on a date, official telephone service will be opened.

Announcement from the Garrison Headquarters: Strictly Prohibiting Extortion Under False Pretenses; Family Members of Offenders Must Not Solicit Bribes; Those Who Dare to Violate Will Be Strictly Investigated 119

Announcement from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters: It has been investigated that the military law office of this headquarters handles cases with the principle of speedy resolution without injustice or leniency. However, in order to discover the truth and avoid unjust leniency, it is necessary to strive for thoroughness in summoning witnesses, investigating arguments, and studying the case. Recently, it has been found that some offenders or their family members, hoping to escape the law or be released early, have engaged in bribery. For example, Zhao F茂, the family member of drug offender Zhao Zhongfan, was defrauded of several hundred yuan while entrusting someone to find a way. All the fraudulent offenders have been arrested and interrogated by this headquarters. This kind of behavior not only wastes money but also violates laws and regulations, amounting to adding crime upon crime, which is both pitiful and detestable. This headquarters enforces the law strictly, and all staff members also cherish self-respect. Those who are guilty will not be allowed to escape the law, and those who are innocent will not be allowed to suffer injustice. There will be no deviations due to the lobbying of offenders or their family members, and bribes will never be accepted to violate the law. Therefore, a special announcement is made to all prisoners in custody: From now on, you must wait patiently for the trial. All family members of offenders must not engage in bribery again. Those who dare to violate will be severely punished. If there are unscrupulous elements who spread rumors under false names and extort money under pretexts, please report them secretly to this headquarters for strict investigation and handling. All must comply. This announcement is made on June 3rd, the 25th year of the Republic of China. Commander Yang Hu.

Representatives of Foundry Workers in the City Petitioned the Party Headquarters Yesterday, Requesting that Employers Be Ordered Not to Arrest Workers 120

According to Da Gong She, the Fuxing Foundry on Qiwu Pu Road in Pudong reported the arrest of worker Ni Lounian to the police, causing a reaction from workers in various foundries throughout the city, who went on strike in succession to show support. After persuasion by personnel from the city party headquarters, work was resumed. However, as the workers' demands had not been resolved, yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, more than 120 representatives from various factories gathered at the city party headquarters to petition. Zhu Rongsheng was elected as the plenipotentiary representative. Li Weixiong, a cadre from the Civil Movement Section of the city party headquarters, received them and expressed acceptance of the workers' demands. They dispersed around 2 o'clock in the afternoon. The petition is recorded as follows: To comply with the request of all representatives and lead the petition. According to the request of the representatives of various factories under the association, on May 26th, at 10 o'clock in the morning, Fan Guoan, the manager of Fuxing Foundry, led police officers into Shenji Foundry without notifying the person in charge of the factory or announcing the reason, and without showing any credentials, suddenly arresting worker Ni Lounian, thereby arousing the public anger of fellow workers in the city, who unanimously went on strike to show support. After reporting to your department for investigation, Mr. Li Weixiong, a representative, investigated the situation on both sides and instructed the representatives to give four points in person: It was determined that the responsibility for this strike event lies with the employer who should be responsible. The arrest of worker Ni Lounian will be assisted and resolved by the city party headquarters according to law. The wage loss caused by the strike due to this incident will be the responsibility of the city party headquarters representative, who will order the employer to give a discretionary amount. The workers must consider the overall situation and resume work together first. At that time, the representatives respected the meaning of the representatives of your department and believed in the prompts of their responsible persons, so they all retreated and persuaded the workers to resume work together first and wait quietly for resolution. However, a week has passed, and this wage has not been handled as instructed, and the workers have questioned one after another, and the representatives have no way to respond. Therefore, they led to your department to petition two items: Order the employer not to use oppressive means in the future, and arrest and detain workers out of suspicion. Wages during the strike period will be paid as usual on a scheduled date. We sincerely ask your department to sympathize with the difficulties of the workers and promptly handle it, which will be convenient for the workers.

The Cotton Control Association Initiates a Jiangbei Cotton Area Inspection Tour, Inviting the Financial Sector to Depart on the Evening of the 10th 121

My country's cotton production is abundant, and Jiangsu is especially so. The various reclamation areas in Jiangbei have vast areas, from Lvsi Town in Nantong to Chenjiagang in Funing, spanning more than 600 li from north to south and about 100 li from east to west. Originally, it was a wasteland for storing grass and boiling salt. Although there are nearly 3.8 million mu of cultivated land, with an annual harvest of 600,000 dan of cotton, there are still more than 10 million mu of wasteland to be developed. Ge Qin, the commissioner of the Nantong District Supervisory Commissioner's Office, considering the importance of its relationship to the Chinese cotton industry, specially consulted with the Cotton Control Association to initiate an invitation to various cotton experts and banks engaged in agricultural finance to send representatives to visit the various reclamation companies. Those invited include the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, the Jiangsu Farmers Bank, the Jin Cheng Bank, the China Farmers Bank, the Four Banks Joint Savings Society, the Chung Nan Bank, the New China Bank, the Kwok Wah Bank, the Continental Bank, The Yieh Yeh Bank, the China National Products Bank, and cotton planting and textile experts from the Cotton Control Association, etc. They will depart from Shanghai on the evening of the 10th of this month, passing through Nantong, Hai'an, Dongtai, Xinyangji, Chenjiayangzi, Baojiadun, etc., for a total journey of about ten days. It is reported that the Jiangsu Provincial Government has also sent five experts in water conservancy, agriculture, and cooperation to join the group and inspect together. It is also reported that Zhu Ziqiao, chairman of the Huainan Reclamation Federation, plans to personally go to receive them.

Chinese Yangtze River Pilots Petition: Transfer Management Authority to the Ministry of Communications; Representatives Went to Nanjing Yesterday; Request Assistance from All Sectors Again 122

Chinese Yangtze River pilots are demanding the return of management authority, the abolition of the Shanghai Pilotage Management Committee, and the transfer of full management authority to the Ministry of Communications. This has been repeatedly called for and detailed in previous reports. It is now learned that the pilots have issued a second circular telegram yesterday, requesting assistance from all sectors, and have sent three representatives, including Feng Fucheng, to Nanjing to petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, and various relevant ministries and committees, in order to realize this as soon as possible, so as to maintain sovereignty and consolidate national defense. The full text of the circular telegram is recorded below: For the appreciation of national party and government organs, various people's organizations, and various newspapers: Since the former Qing government trusted foreign advisors and abandoned pilotage authority, in the seventh year of Tongzhi, Robert Hart, the British customs commissioner of Jianghai Customs, formulated the General Regulations for Pilotage, stipulating that foreigners could serve as pilots in our country. In addition, Daniel, a British shipping commissioner of the Shanghai River Shipping Bureau, assigned the waterway from Tongsha to Shanghai to a foreign pilotage organization for exclusive management, from which sovereignty was lost, foreign advisors manipulated things, and the Chinese people suffered. The pilotage industry declined tragically. We eagerly hoped that the government would take it back and manage it itself. Fortunately, our national government abolished the General Regulations for Pilotage formulated by Robert Hart in the twelfth year of the Republic of China and strived to recover pilotage authority. The Chinese people deeply rejoiced at being freed from the control of foreign advisors. Later, the Ministries of Finance, Navy, Communications, and the General Staff jointly formed the Shanghai Pilotage Management Committee as an organization to manage foreign pilots. The Chinese people were delighted with this measure, believing that the Chinese people's pilotage industry would have a more reliable guarantee and would be able to flourish, so as to maintain sovereignty and consolidate national defense. Unexpectedly, since the establishment of the committee, all measures have been contrary to their purpose, turning against each other. Controlling Chinese pilots on the Yangtze River seemed to be the sole responsibility of the committee. The committee dared to act perversely, probably because the government did not consider it fully when establishing the committee, resulting in this problem. Although the committee was jointly organized by representatives from various departments, the Interim Regulations for Pilotage Management promulgated in the 22nd year of the Republic of China designated the customs patrol and river shipping bureaus as representatives of the Ministry of Finance and concurrently served as chairman and members, and representatives of foreign chambers of commerce participated in it, so that our sacred sovereignty still fell into the hands of foreign advisors. It is regrettable to say and causes anger to think about. Investigating the pilotage of ships entering and leaving ports and navigating rivers and seas is related to the mission of transportation and the security of national defense. All countries in the world strictly guard their borders and prohibit foreigners. Only our country trusts foreign advisors, erring once with Robert Hart and again with Daniel. Now, the chairman of the Shanghai Pilotage Management Committee, Cornell, is trying to control our people, and his intention is even more vicious than that of Robert Hart and Daniel. The danger of the matter is unsurpassed. In the past, French warships attacked the Min River port and Japanese warships penetrated the Liu River. The past events are not far away and can serve as a warning. Our association is saddened by what it sees and is duty-bound to safeguard sovereignty and consolidate national defense. In addition to having repeatedly presented to the relevant departments and painfully explained the pros and cons, urging rescue, the fundamental solution is to immediately abolish the Pilotage Management Committee and change it to be examined and issued licenses by the Ministry of Communications, and then managed and guided by the local maritime administration bureaus. The Legislative Yuan should promulgate the Pilotage Law to benefit the competent authorities and pilots, and establish a pilotage school to cultivate pilotage talents. At the same time, we should dismiss foreign pilots and recover pilotage rights, so that the Chinese people's pilotage industry can prosper and the gateway to the rivers and seas can be consolidated. Even if the aggressors have strong ships and cannons, they cannot enter our gateway, which will greatly benefit national defense. Although there are no treaty restrictions on banning foreign pilots, but the habit has been around for a long time, and it is not easy to ban them, and we are afraid that it will affect diplomacy. Our association is also well aware of this. How can we over-request the government? However, giving up eating because of choking is not the way to national rejuvenation. We must seek solutions through other means. Without affecting diplomacy or the livelihoods of foreign pilots currently serving, and while maintaining our sovereignty, the government should issue an order to all foreign pilots to apply to our competent authorities for examination and registration. After our government examines and approves foreign personnel, it will issue licenses, stipulate the number of people, and restrict the replacement of foreign pilots after death or resignation. Then, in one or two decades, foreign pilots in our country can be completely eliminated, sovereignty can be recovered, and national defense can be guaranteed. Therefore, at this time of severe national crisis, when the nation is seeking to survive, we offer this one idea to the government for adoption. In addition to sending representatives to petition, we are sending another telegram, hoping that everyone will agree and assist in the process, and work together to promote its realization. National defense will be fortunate, and the people will be fortunate. The telegram is urgent, and we are eagerly awaiting your response. Sincerely, the Chinese Yangtze River Pilots Association.

Ministry of Industry Responds to the Hankou Chamber of Commerce, Explaining the Tung Oil Improvement Plan: Official-Merchant Cooperation Is Not Control, and Oil Merchants' Suspicions Are Self-Defeating 124

The Ministry of Industry, in view of the inconsistent quality of my country's tung oil exports, errors in delivery, and the unpredictable fluctuations in market prices, which have caused foreign manufacturers to be wary, and the fact that various European and American countries have had good results in experimental tung tree planting in recent years, if my country does not seek to improve the production and sales of tung oil, it will gradually lose its foreign market. Therefore, it has specially joined with the provinces of Sichuan, Hubei, Hunan, Anhui, and Zhejiang, which produce tung oil, to organize the China Vegetable Oil Factory to implement an entire improvement plan, and invited merchants to participate in share capital and cooperate earnestly. The detailed methods have been repeatedly recorded in various newspapers. It is now learned from relevant sources that Hankou oil merchants are deeply suspicious of this plan. Those who do not understand the government's intentions even believe that it is a trade control, and they are shocked to inform each other. The oil merchants petitioned the Hankou Municipal Chamber of Commerce to present to the Ministry of Industry, requesting an explanation of the provisions of Article 4 of the organizational outline of the Vegetable Oil Factory. It is now learned that the Ministry has replied to the Hankou Market Chamber of Commerce on the 2nd of this month. The original telegram is as follows: "Hankou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, viewed. The Ministry, together with the provinces of Sichuan, Zhejiang, Hubei, Hunan, etc., established the Vegetable Oil Factory for the purpose of improving the quality of tung oil and standardizing product standards. The improvement method is to cooperate with oil merchants to organize a company jointly run by officials and merchants. It does not restrict the freedom to buy and sell tung oil, nor does it contain the meaning of government control. Outsiders who do not understand the truth have actually misinterpreted the sale of tung oil, which is inconsistent with the facts. Tung oil is an important product of our country, a major export, and the oil-producing area is very wide. In order to seek national unity and solidarity, we specially initiated the establishment of this factory, promoted by the government, and not to exclude oil merchants and monopolize sales by the government. As for the original Article 4 of the regulations, which stipulates that no other oil factories with the same operation may exist, it is only for the sake of future standardization. Oil merchants in the city have no reason to be suspicious. Now the preparatory office of the factory has been established. How the original oil merchants can participate in cooperation can be discussed at length. Please instruct them to negotiate with the preparatory office of the factory and do not listen to rumors and cause misunderstandings. Ministry of Industry, winter seal." According to the spokesperson of the preparatory committee of the China Vegetable Oil Factory, the benefits of Chinese merchants participating in the factory plan are as follows: 1. The factory will first inspect the oil quality of the crude oil it receives. Inferior quality will be rejected, and superior quality will be rewarded, which can prevent counterfeiting and improve quality. 2. With centralized processing, the quality can be completely standardized, establishing credit abroad, and the trade status will gradually be consolidated. 3. At present, Chinese merchants have very few oil pool equipment, and acting as an agent for storage and refining can facilitate large and small oil merchants in the interior. 4. When crude oil is delivered to the factory, the factory will issue "inventory certificates" at any time. Oil merchants can use this certificate to make deposits or remittances to banks and money shops, and obtain low-interest funds from banks, which can relieve the pain of high-interest loans for Chinese merchants. 5. Spot transactions can be based on net oil as the standard, and the quality and delivery date are guaranteed. 6. Centralized insurance declarations, etc., can reduce the costs. 7. Issuing certificates can prevent internal fraud and establish external credit. 8. Centralized storage can count the quantity, and transactions and operations can be grasped, and market prices may gradually stabilize. 9. Refining before storage will prevent the formation of dregs. 10. Storing in new-style oil pools will avoid oil loss, and merchants can wait for prices to sell. 11. Selling tung oil to exporters can avoid the trouble of inspecting oil dregs, and the costs can be reduced. 12. The transportation of crude oil involves large quantities and heavy charges (such as freight, tariffs, insurance, etc.), while net oil is more economical. It is also said that the factory's recruitment prospectus has been established and is attached as follows:

China Vegetable Oil Factory Co., Ltd. Prospectus Tung oil is a special product of my country and a major export. In order to improve quality and improve management, we have initiated the organization of the China Vegetable Oil Factory, specializing in the agency storage and refining of tung oil and facilitating transportation and sales as the main business. In addition to drafting regulations and submitting them to the 622nd meeting of the Executive Yuan for approval, a recruitment prospectus is specially formulated as follows: 1. The factory is organized as a joint-stock limited company, jointly run by officials and merchants. 2. Official shares of the factory will be separately allocated by the Ministry of Industry and the provinces of Zhejiang, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, etc. 3. The company's headquarters will be located in Shanghai as the general office, and factories will be established in the tung oil producing areas in turn. 4. The total capital is 2 million yuan, divided into 20,000 shares, each share being 100 yuan. Half of the payment will be collected first. 5. In addition to the official shares being determined to be half, in order to promote cooperation between officials and the people and to popularize the interests of all sectors, 10,000 shares are specially reserved for raising merchant shares. 6. The stock is registered and divided into four types: five shares, ten shares, fifty shares, and one hundred shares. 7. Stockholders are limited to those with Republic of China nationality. 8. Commercial shares receive an official interest of 8%, and official shares receive an official interest of 6%. If the settlement surplus is insufficient for commercial shares to receive official interest, the Ministry of Industry will pay 6% interest or make up the difference according to 6%. 9. Shareholders with 60 or more commercial shares are eligible to be elected as directors. With the approval of the Executive Yuan transferred by the Ministry of Industry, no other organizations with the same business are allowed to exist in the country regarding the storage, refining, and pressing of tung oil. The temporary preparatory office of the factory is located in the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry in Shanghai, and preparatory branch offices are established in the construction halls of the four provinces of Zhejiang, Hubei, Hunan, and Sichuan to handle all preparatory matters. If there are any contact matters, you can send a letter or consult with each office separately. Subscribers should fill in the subscription form, pay the stock payment according to the shares, and obtain a formal receipt. The deadline for raising shares, receiving payments, and the deadline date will be published in the newspaper. All items not specified in this prospectus shall be handled in accordance with the company's articles of association. Founders: Ministry of Industry, Preparatory Committee, Wu Tingju, Director of the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province, Liu Zhenpeng, Director of the Construction Department of Hubei Province, Yu Jiechuan, Director of the Construction Department of Hunan Province, Lu Zuofu, Director of the Construction Department of Sichuan Province, Zhang Jiazhu, Deputy Director of the International Trade Bureau, Chairman of the Preparatory Committee.

Female Workers at Shanghai Textile and Dyeing Factory Once Engaged in a Go-Slow Yesterday Morning, Expressing Support for Dismissed Workers, and Resumed Work After Persuasion from the Factory 125

According to Da Gong She, Shanghai Textile Printing & Dyeing Co., located at 1382 Huade Road, Pudong, found in the middle of last week that some female workers in the textile department, under the pretext of poor treatment, attempted to jointly strike. After investigation by the factory, more than 20 female workers who were the leaders were dismissed. After being laid off, the female workers had difficulties making a living and often pestered the factory. Yesterday morning at 6 o'clock, more than 300 female workers in the textile department of the factory went on a go-slow to show their support for the dismissed workers. The factory could not persuade them, so they called the Yulin Road police station in the jurisdiction and sent more than 60 police cars and detectives to suppress them. At about 7 o'clock, after further persuasion from the factory, all of them resumed work as usual.

Special Commissioner of the Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee Continues to Report on Inspection of Relief Work in Jiangsu and Shandong 129

The Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee on Renji Road, considering that the disaster areas in northern Jiangsu, northern Anhui, and Shandong are in a critical state of food shortage and widespread suffering, allocated 100,000 yuan to the branch associations in the areas to carry out both emergency relief and rehabilitation, in addition to monitoring everything by local Chinese and Western personnel, and specially sent two commissioners, Yu and Zheng, to various places to seriously inspect the situation, which was recorded in previous reports. The association has received a report from Commissioner Yu, stating that the Xuyi County branch of the relief committee has completed the inspection and receipt of complaints in the first district, Xinyi, and other eight villages, and has provided relief to 1,179 households, with 5,895 people of all ages, issuing national currency of 2,927 yuan. Following this, the Tushan branch of Pizhou County, its fourth district, including Qixin, a total of 30 guarantors, has 1,833 households receiving relief, with 8,952 people of all ages. Relief tickets are divided into 1 yuan, 2 yuan, and 3 yuan, with a total amount of 2,935 yuan issued. There is still a lot of accumulated water along the way, and the places that have not receded are still numerous. Wheat seedlings were sown too late, or there are harvests, but they are very limited. Sorghum and pearl millet were severely damaged by soil insects, adding disaster upon disaster. The situation is extremely tragic, etc. Commissioner Zheng reported that he has completed the inspection of Jining (Shandong) and arrived in Jiaxiang County. The emergency relief has been inspected and completed, totaling 50 villages, and 4,250 yuan of relief funds have been issued. The county suffered the most severe disaster because the Yellow River breached its banks last autumn, flooding western Shandong. The Yellow River from Ju and Wen counties to the east flowed through this county into Nanyang Lake, so it suffered the most damage. The disaster area is about 30 li from east to west and 70 li from north to south, with about 5,000 hectares of flooded fields and more than 300 villages flooded, affecting more than 140,000 victims. Houses collapsed, and property losses amounted to about 2.5 million yuan. Witnessing the villages, most of the autumn wheat was not planted, and the victims are filling their stomachs with tree leaves and grass roots, which is extremely tragic, etc.

Zhou Yisu Declares His Withdrawal from the Production Party 133

According to the Central News Agency, the young man Zhou Yisu, realizing that the Production Party is deceiving the public and intends to disrupt national security, resolutely declared his withdrawal and issued a declaration of withdrawal from the Production Party, stating that the Chinese nation is currently facing an unprecedented crisis, but we look forward to the future of China and will never fall into a pessimistic and desperate situation. Because we have a glorious and brilliant history of five thousand years and a population of 455 million, such a large country known for its culture is by no means comparable to the small country of Abyssinia. Since the Opium War, China has repeatedly been on the verge of danger due to foreign aggression, but it has always been able to turn danger into safety, and the national destiny has continued until now, still standing on the East Asian continent. This is no accident. At the end of the late Qing Dynasty, the monarch was weak and the ministers were dark, and internal affairs were not cultivated, which led to foreign powers taking advantage of the situation. The national vitality was on the verge of extinction. However, although foreign enemies were strong, even during the corrupt days of the abdicated Qing Dynasty, they could not destroy China. Moreover, today, official governance is enlightened, the national foundation is solid, and construction is advancing rapidly. Our Chairman Chiang is in sole charge, directing decisively. Domestic banditry is on the decline, and civil wars are gradually being quelled. Pacifying the interior is the way to resist foreign aggression. Recuperation and education, lying on firewood and tasting gall, sincere unity, and the essence of striving are the times. Is there any reason for China to perish? "To resist the enemy and avoid regretting, we must first have a correct assessment, and to restore the nation, we must also have a necessary process. Let us ask, based on the current situation in our country, how can we compare with other countries in terms of national strength, financial resources, or military strength? At this time, if there is no sufficient and solid preparation, and a unanimous determination from top to bottom, to rashly fight is like throwing an egg against a stone. As for the work of national restoration, it must go through at least three stages. First, we must restore our country's inherent morality and culture, promote national essence, encourage integrity, and reject foreign hand-shrinking class struggle and various evils, so that 400 million people will be of one mind and have the same national thoughts and consciousness. Then the national spirit can surge and be unstoppable. Second, we must improve our country's production and construction. The reason for our country's weakness is the backwardness of industry, the failure of industry and commerce, the lack of developed transportation, and the inability to exploit mining. At present, to save weakness and seek strength, we can only actively engage in material construction, revitalize national industry, build railways and highways, develop underground treasures, and work hard to transform our country into a modern country. Food and clothing before soldiers, national wealth before national strength, ancient teachings are obvious, and improving production and construction is the most basic work of national rejuvenation. Third, we must promote military national education. Now all countries in the world are talking about military affairs and expanding armaments. Standing in the 20th century today, we feel terrified and fearful. To defend against aggression and strive for strength, we can only increase armaments and promote military national education, so that everyone has a martial spirit and a healthy body. With one heart and one mind, we will be able to wash away national humiliation and turn weakness into strength in the blink of an eye. From the above, it can be seen that without sufficient preparation and the mobilization of the entire nation, we must never engage in resistance to the enemy and resisting humiliation. Otherwise, we will take the nation as a sacrifice and put the country in a state of eternal destruction. As for the work of national revival, it cannot be accomplished overnight. It must go through a preparatory stage and a long-term recuperation and education work. It must also be under the firm and unwavering leadership of the wise and responsible authorities to lay a safe cornerstone. Now, some frustrated bureaucrats, politicians, and reactionaries often criticize the government authorities on the issue of resistance to the enemy. It is either unfounded or intended to undermine the prestige of the government and divide the united front of the entire nation. All reactionary groups, such as the Communist Party, the Social Democratic Party, and the Third Party, are now spreading their tongues and trumpeting the claim of "resistance to aggression and saving the country." Little do they know that the Labor Party uses the theory of class struggle to advocate national revolution, which cannot cover up its deceptive effect. The red lackeys of the Social Democratic Party and the Third Party, etc., are acting as accomplices for the party and reversing black and white, which are also moths that obstruct the national revolution. Only by standing firmly under the leadership of the central responsible authorities can we shoulder this arduous task of restoring the nation, saving the country, and seeking survival. Only by trusting the current government's foreign policy and the supreme leader's effective measures for the political situation can we save the country's misfortune. I have withdrawn from the "National Revolutionary Alliance" because I do not want to be a tool for some frustrated warlords and bureaucrats, helping the wicked to do evil. Now I have become a sincere supporter of the current government, because I have confirmed that the policies implemented by the current government have indeed entered an important stage of national revival. Saving the country does not advocate empty talk. Today, the government is immersed in construction, and the spirit of lying on firewood and tasting gall has laid the foundation for a century-long plan for saving the country and seeking survival. I hope that the revolutionary youth of the country will unite under the leadership of the government and move forward.

Funeral Permit Fee in the French Concession: Five Yuan Minimum, Additional Fee After Eight Days 135

The French Consulate in Shanghai recently issued Decree No. 122, stipulating that the coffin of a person who dies in the French Concession must be moved out within seven days. If they wish to stay at home, they must apply to the Health Bureau for a permit. The permit fee is five yuan per sheet for seven to fifteen days, and ten yuan per sheet for fifteen to thirty days. Those who do not move out after the deadline and apply to keep the coffin will be charged five yuan from the first to the fifteenth day and ten yuan from the fifteenth to the thirtieth day.

French Concession Taxpayers' Association Negotiates the Abolition of the Sanitation Fee; The License of Tongxing Fuguanqi Store Was Taken Away; Sends a Letter to the Taxpayers' Association to Protest to the French Municipal Council 136

The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association recently received a letter from the Second District Branch of the Citizens' Federation, stating that Wu Futian, the owner of Tongxing Fuguanqi Store at No. 484 Fahua Min Road, reported that on May 28, the French Municipal Council suddenly sent a large number of Chinese and Western detectives to his residence and shop, saying that there were also Fuguanqi objects in the residence and that he must also pay a sanitation license fee and investigate. He was very surprised to hear this. Since the objects in his shop were not related to hygiene, paying the sanitation fee was already beyond reason, but he had been paying it painfully until now. How could there be additional complications? It is normal for the remaining objects in the shop to be placed in the residence. If he is forced to pay for a license, it is extremely unreasonable. Therefore, he was unwilling to pay, but the detectives used strong-arm tactics and forcibly took away the original license of his shop and copied the door number back to the police station, and then threatened to issue a fine. The detectives are so rampant and unscrupulous that I am afraid that he is not the only merchant who has been harmed. Therefore, he has no choice but to ask the association to help him and forward his protest to the French Municipal Council to strictly negotiate and abolish this harsh tax as soon as possible to avoid disturbances. According to this, it is appropriate to convey it and hope that he will propose a negotiation. After receiving the letter, the association has sent personnel to investigate and verified the facts and has submitted a negotiation to the French Municipal Council.

Shanghai-Beijing Through Train Will Set Up Third-Class Sleeping Cars; One Yuan or One Yuan and Fifty Cents Per Night; Actively Preparing 142

Since the implementation of the Shanghai-Beijing through train, passengers have found it convenient. However, due to the long distance and the 48-hour travel time, the Ministry of Railways has set up sleeper berths in the first and second-class cars to allow passengers to sleep, but the third-class cars are lacking. Public Concession Authorities Strive to Improve Traffic; Revise Traffic Regulations; Restrict Vehicle Parking 143

Regarding restricting vehicles from parking on the roadside to reduce street congestion, in April last year, the Chief of the Police Department of the Public Works Bureau suggested to the Board of Directors that the parking of vehicles on congested streets should be further restricted. The Board of Directors approved this in principle and planned to implement it at any time after nine months with a sixty-day notice. The names of the congested streets and the daytime restrictions could be increased and modified as needed. At that time, the streets and times of implementation were announced. Later, the Chief of the Police Department took advantage of a long vacation to return to his country to investigate foreign traffic management methods for reference. When the Chief returned to Shanghai after his vacation, he submitted a second report to the Board of Directors. According to his observations abroad, the source of traffic congestion in the city lies in the unrestricted parking of vehicles on narrower streets. Even in the Public Concession, the streets are gradually widening, and traffic should not be hindered. However, the arbitrary and long-term parking of vehicles has created a situation of street congestion. This situation is particularly obvious in the central district. Therefore, according to the opinion of the Chief of the Police Department, to rectify street traffic, it is necessary to start with banning parking, and this matter should not be delayed any longer. Otherwise, procrastination will gradually become unmanageable. Therefore, the Public Works Bureau recently decided to revise the traffic regulations based on the following principles: The existence of streets is to ensure smooth traffic. The parking of vehicles should be in permitted locations, that is, locations designated by the police authorities as not hindering free traffic. Vehicles should be allowed to park temporarily, except in "no parking" locations that obstruct traffic or are specially prohibited. In any part of a street, parking is not allowed if it obstructs the free flow of vehicles. In accordance with the practices of other cities, all locations where vehicles can be parked will be marked, and the current "no parking" signs will be abolished. In addition, vehicles may park temporarily, except in locations where "no parking" signs are erected and in locations where parking is specially prohibited. The parking time in the central downtown area is limited to one hour, but in certain locations, it will be shortened as appropriate. In streets that are not specifically marked, the parking time may be slightly extended within the scope of not hindering traffic. The names of streets where parking is allowed for one hour may be increased as appropriate in the future. The streets with parking restrictions have been published in yesterday's English gazette of the Public Works Bureau. In addition, the traffic routes at the Bund and Yangjingbang are currently very chaotic and will be improved in the future. The Deputy Director of the Public Works Department has drafted a plan and will implement it soon. In addition, the Suzhou Road riverbank can be developed into a number of parking spaces, but the work will not be carried out until the restrictions are not severe. It is said that the above-mentioned vehicle restriction measures will be implemented three months later, that is, starting from September 5.

Heroin Trafficking Operation Cracked on Danshui Road, Undercover Detectives Posing as Customers, Confiscating More Than Twenty-Five Ounces of Heroin, Police Observe Not Within the Means of Chinese Nationals 152

Detectives Yang Zhaoqing, Wang Rulin, Guo Ruiquan, and others from the Anti-Narcotics Department of the General Patrol Room recently cracked a heroin trafficking operation at No. 11 Lishui Lane, No. 24 Danshui Road, and arrested Cao Yunyou from Taizhou, Wang Ziru from Haimen, Wang Bao, a woman from Suzhou, and Wang Qingyi from Taizhou, and confiscated 25 taels of heroin, plus a small packet, a ledger, and a scale, all of which were taken to Chengdu Road Patrol Room and detained separately. Cao then gave him a small packet of samples and agreed on a price of 25 yuan per tael, but he would not sell in small quantities, with a minimum of 25 taels, totaling 625 yuan in national currency, and agreed to exchange the money and goods at 2 p.m. Detective Wang reported back to Western Detective Chief and requested the court to issue a search warrant and cooperate with other detectives to wait around Cao's house. On the one hand, Detective Wang still entered the house, and Cao sent his uncle Wang Ziru out. Half an hour later, he came with Wang Qingyi and met with Detective Wang. Wang Qingyi again sent Wang Ziru out. At 3:40 p.m., he returned with a woman, Wang Bao, who was holding a box of Great Britain brand cigarette paper, containing 25 taels of heroin. Cao immediately asked Detective Wang to hand over 625 yuan in cash. Detective Wang, wanting to test whether the paper bag contained genuine goods, took a glass of water, and Wang Bao used a needle to pierce it, extracted a little, and poured it into the water. At that time, Chinese and Western detectives rushed in to arrest them. The patrol room found that No. 11 Lishui Lane was only a liaison office. If there were customers, they would go out to pick it up. And they observed that the heroin's paper packaging was tight and sealed with lead, which was not within the means of Chinese nationals. Therefore, they requested an extension in order to investigate the source of the drugs. Cao Yunyou confessed that the heroin was brought by Wang Bao, Wang Ziru was his wife's younger brother, and Wang Qingyi lived at No. 22 Liji Lane, Zilaishui Street, French Concession, and came to my place to play yesterday. Wang Ziru confessed that his brother-in-law instructed him to call Wang Qingyi. He happened to meet him on the road. Wang Bao was Wang Qingyi's concubine. He did not know the value of the heroin Wang brought. Wang Bao confessed that she had known Wang Qingyi before and was now a prostitute at Rui Xiang Yuan in the French Concession (stage name Hua Yuanyuan Lao Si). Yesterday, she met Wang Ziru on the road and saw him holding a paper box. Because Wang owed me 10 yuan in French currency, I asked for it. Wang then instructed me to go home with him to get it, and when I got to the door, he handed me the paper box to hold temporarily, not knowing it was drugs, etc. Wang Qingyi's confession was evasive, saying that he came to Shanghai from Taizhou to find Cao Yunyou for only two days and knew nothing about the rest. Judge Huang Risheng verified the confessions and ordered the four defendants to be detained pending a further hearing on the 11th of this month.

Chen Zun'gui and Yu Qingsong Went to Japan Last Night to Observe the Solar Eclipse, Chen Discussed the Image of the Total Solar Eclipse in Detail, the Sun Was Obscured and the Day Suddenly Turned into Night 153

The big event in the astronomical world this year is the total solar eclipse on June 19. The Astronomical Research Institute of the Central Research Institute of our country also sent special personnel to observe it in Boli, the Soviet Union, and Hokkaido, Japan. Observers Zhang Yuche and Li Yan, who went to Boli, had already set off for the Soviet Union a few days ago. Chen Zun'gui and Yu Qingsong, two solar eclipse observers who went to Hokkaido, Japan, came to Shanghai yesterday morning and took the Japanese mail ship Chichibu Maru to Japan at 12 o'clock that night. A reporter from Shenshi News Agency made a special visit to the hotel yesterday to interview them, and the following is a record of the conversation:

Meaning, Location, and Process of the Solar Eclipse

Chen first described the significance of a total solar eclipse, saying that the earth revolves around the sun once a year, and the moon revolves around the earth once a month. The two rotate continuously, year after year. It takes about 400 years to discover a total solar eclipse at a fixed location. The locations through which this year's total solar eclipse passes begin in the Caspian Sea in Europe, then pass through Siberia, Chita, and other places in the Soviet Union, to Qigan and Huma in Heilongjiang, China, then to Boli in the Soviet Union, and Hokkaido, Japan, and finally into the Pacific Ocean.

The Earth is Dark During a Total Solar Eclipse

Around 3 p.m. this month, all of Mari, Boli, and Hokkaido are locations through which the total solar eclipse passes. The total solar eclipse lasts only one minute and fifty-seven seconds. At this time, the sun, moon, and earth are in perfect alignment. The bright sun hanging high in the sky is suddenly obscured by the moon, and the earth immediately becomes dark, as if it were a full moon night. The twinkling stars are terrified and the birds and animals roar. We look up at the sky again and see the black shadow of the moon obscuring the sun, with the light of the lunar corona shooting out around the moon. This phenomenon lasts for one minute and fifty-seven seconds, after which the moon gradually moves past the obscured sun and returns to its original state.

Observe the Partial Solar Eclipse with Blackened Glass

There are three types of solar eclipses. A total solar eclipse is when the sun is completely obscured by the moon, a partial solar eclipse is when only a part is obscured, and an annular solar eclipse is when the center of the sun is obscured. Around 3 p.m. on June 19, locations not in the path of the total solar eclipse, such as Shanghai and Nanjing, can see the image of a partial solar eclipse by covering the eyes with glass lightly coated with black ink to observe the sun.

The Mission of Observing the Total Solar Eclipse

Chen continued, that this total solar eclipse is highly valued by countries all over the world. Astronomers from various countries have gathered in Boli in the Soviet Union and Hokkaido in Japan. The mission of observing the total solar eclipse is to study the shape of the total solar eclipse and take photographs. The other is to visit the instruments used by various countries to observe the total solar eclipse and how Japan treats inspectors from various countries, so as to learn from it for the total solar eclipse in our country in 1941.

Prediction of the Total Solar Eclipse in Our Country

The total solar eclipse in our country was discovered once in 1542 (the 21st year of the Jiajing reign of the Ming Dynasty). After about 400 years, a total solar eclipse will be discovered again in 1941 (the 30th year of the Republic of China). The area through which it passes starts from Xinjiang, passes through Gansu, Shaanxi, Hubei, Jiangxi, and reaches the Fujian-Zhejiang border, and enters the Pacific Ocean.

Observation Specialist Departed for Japan Last Night

Chen concluded that our country's observation team to Japan consists of three people. Yu Qingsong and I are carrying more than ten pieces of observation equipment, such as telescopes, chronometers, and movie cameras. We came to Shanghai from Beijing on the evening of the 3rd, and took the Japanese ship Chichibu Maru to Japan on the night of the 4th. We should arrive in Hokkaido around the 11th. There is also a student studying in Japan. After observing the total solar eclipse on the 16th, we will visit observatories in Tokyo and other places, and we will be able to return to China by the end of this month.

Page 14

Rampant Abduction in Shanghai, Cracks in Taiyuan and Yida Ships, Male and Female Abductors Transferred to Court for Interrogation 154

Two Boys Sleeping Together Under a Quilt, Investigators Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang of the China Women and Children Relief Association, together with detectives Wang Haiquan, Qu Heqi, Xu Juelu, and others from the Customs Water Police Station, went to the Taiyuan ship of the Taikoo Company's Nanyang line at the Bund in the French Concession to investigate at around 4 a.m. yesterday. The five-year-old child spoke with a Suzhou accent, and the six-year-old child spoke with a Changzhou accent, which was obviously contradictory. At this time, the young woman suddenly went to the toilet to relieve herself and never returned. The old woman, along with the two suspects, was taken to the Water Police Station. Today, Bao Lin said that he would take me to Qingdao to find business, but I didn't know I was going to be trafficked. The arrested male defendant confessed that his false name was He Rongxiu, his real name was Zhen Dalun, and he was from Shandong. He had been a police officer in Wuxi. He stammered and could not answer the rest of the questions. One female defendant, named Wu Zhaoshang, 29 years old, from Jiangbei, gave a cunning confession. When the other two women were interrogated, they both claimed that they had also been abducted. One was named Zhao Xiaomei, 19 years old, from Jiangbei. She used to work in Wuxi. Two weeks ago, Mo Chunlin, whom I knew, sent me a letter from Shanghai, inviting me to Shanghai to find a job. The next morning, he introduced me to the defendant He Ronghua, and we became lovers. I heard them discuss the word "trafficking" (commonly known as abducting women), and only then did I realize I had been deceived. Another was named Gu Damei, from Pudong. Wu Zhaodi and others persuaded me to do the business of "selling people" (prostitution), first selling me to a brothel in Qingdao, and then escaping within a week, commonly known as "running away." I am very willing to do this. The detectives told her that after being sold to a brothel, someone would watch her all day long, and even if she made a living by selling her body, her lifelong happiness would be completely ruined. Damei realized that she had been deceived by the defendants. The police chief, finding that three abducted women had been found in one case, notified the Women and Children Relief Association to send two investigators, Chen and Lin, to the case, and they were all transferred to the Local Court for interrogation.

Woman Accused of Abusing Her Own Daughter, Her Husband Also Argues for Legal Action After Repeatedly Failing to Persuade Her 155

The Chinese Children's Welfare Association sent a staff member, Zhao Jian, to the Old Gate Police Station at 10 a.m. the day before yesterday, reporting that Liu Ren, a Ningbo woman living at No. 428, Edward Road, was abusing her nine-year-old daughter, Liu Derong, and requested an investigation. Chinese Detective He Renrui and Western Detective Aston went to investigate and learned that Liu Ren's husband, Liu Jisheng, was a typesetter. Derong was born to Liu Ren. Recently, she beat her daughter with a wooden stick, tied her hands with a rope, and did not allow her to eat, causing her body to be covered with injuries and her eyes and forehead to be swollen. The situation was very tragic. They immediately arrested Liu Ren and sent the girl to Guangren Hospital for examination, which confirmed that she had been injured. Liu Ren's husband, Liu Jisheng, also said that he had repeatedly tried to persuade her without success, so he advocated legal action. Yesterday morning, the police station sent Liu Ren to the First Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Lawyer Wang Yaotang of the police station explained the situation, requesting that she be punished in accordance with Article 286, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law for abusing boys and girls under the age of sixteen, thereby hindering their natural development. Then Liu Derong filed a complaint, stating that she had been abused by her mother from time to time, and showed the court the swollen injuries on her arms and legs. Then Liu Jisheng, the second landlord Zhu Wenyue, the owner of the Yongli Straw Paper Shop, and the cohabitant Mo Wentao successively testified to Liu Ren's abusive behavior. When questioned, Liu Ren also admitted that she had beaten her daughter, but only to discipline her for constantly stirring up trouble. Judge Feng Shide ruled that the facts were clear and ordered the start of the debate. Police Lawyer Wang stated that the defendant's criminal behavior was very clear, but the defendant's motive was to discipline her children, but the method of discipline was too excessive. Also, the defendant had never been punished before, so he requested that a suspended sentence be announced at the time of sentencing, giving her an opportunity to rehabilitate herself. Judge Feng then ordered Liu Ren to be remanded in custody and scheduled the verdict for this Saturday.
